      Text001@1100525000 : TextConst 'DEU=Lagerzeit,Cash-flow;ENU=Age Composition,Cash Flow;NLD=Ouderdomsanalyse,Kasstroom;NOR=Alderskomposisjon,Kontantstrõm;SVE=èlderskomposition,Kassaflîde';
      Text002@1100525002 : TextConst 'DEU=Buchungsdatum,FÑlligkeitsdatum,Belegdatum;ENU=Posting Date,Due Date,Document Date;NLD=Boekingsdatum,Vervaldatum,Documentdatum;NOR=Bokfõringsdato,forfallsdato,Dokumentdato;SVE=Bokfîringsdatum,Fîrfallodatum,Dokumentdatum';

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter1@1100525000() : Text;

      IF Vendor.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN

    PROCEDURE FillPeriodInfo@1210190017();
    BEGIN
      PeriodStartDateArray[1] := 0D;
      CASE ReportType OF
        ReportType::"Age Composition":
          BEGIN
            SwitchSignDateFormula(PeriodLength);
            PeriodStartDateArray[NoOfPeriods] := ReferenceDate;
            FOR PeriodNo := (NoOfPeriods - 1) DOWNTO 2 DO
              PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo] := CALCDATE(PeriodLength, PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo+1]);
          END;
        ReportType::"Cash Flow":
          BEGIN
            PeriodStartDateArray[2] := ReferenceDate;
            FOR PeriodNo := 3 TO NoOfPeriods DO
              PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo] := CALCDATE(PeriodLength, PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo-1]);
          END;
      END;

      FOR PeriodNo := 1 TO (NoOfPeriods - 1) DO
        PeriodEndDateArray[PeriodNo] := PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo+1] - 1;
      PeriodEndDateArray[NoOfPeriods] := 99991231D;

      CASE ReportType OF
        ReportType::"Age Composition":
          BEGIN
            PeriodDaysTxtArray[1] := '> ' + FORMAT(ReferenceDate - PeriodEndDateArray[1] - 1);
            FOR PeriodNo := 2 TO (NoOfPeriods-1) DO
              PeriodDaysTxtArray[PeriodNo] :=
                FORMAT(ReferenceDate - PeriodEndDateArray[PeriodNo]) + ' - ' +
                FORMAT(ReferenceDate - PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo]);
            PeriodDaysTxtArray[NoOfPeriods] := '< 1';
          END;
        ReportType::"Cash Flow":
          BEGIN
            PeriodDaysTxtArray[1] := '< 1';
            FOR PeriodNo := 2 TO (NoOfPeriods-1) DO
              PeriodDaysTxtArray[PeriodNo] :=
                FORMAT(PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo] - ReferenceDate + 1) + ' - ' +
                FORMAT(PeriodEndDateArray[PeriodNo] - ReferenceDate + 1);
            PeriodDaysTxtArray[NoOfPeriods] := '> ' + FORMAT(PeriodStartDateArray[NoOfPeriods] - ReferenceDate);
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SwitchSignDateFormula@1210190004(VAR IOPeriodLength@1210190000 : DateFormula);
    VAR
      Len@1210190004 : Integer;
      I@1210190003 : Integer;
      Char@1210190002 : Text[1];
      PeriodLengthTxt@1210190001 : Text[100];
    BEGIN
      //* In een DateFormula kunnen geen haakjes gebruikt worden (deze woren automatisch weer weggehaald) daarom werkt
      //* de volgende constructie niet: DateFormula := -(DateFormula)
      //* Dus alle tekens omkeren (als eerste positie geen '+' of '-' dan '-' toevoegen op eerste positie)

      PeriodLengthTxt := FORMAT(IOPeriodLength);
      Len := STRLEN(PeriodLengthTxt);
      FOR I := 1 TO (Len - 1) DO BEGIN
        Char := COPYSTR(PeriodLengthTxt, I, 1);
        IF Char = '+' THEN
          Char := '-'
        ELSE BEGIN
          IF Char = '-' THEN
            Char := '+';
        END;
        IF (Char = '+') OR (Char = '-') THEN BEGIN
          IF I = 1 THEN
            PeriodLengthTxt := Char + COPYSTR(PeriodLengthTxt, (I + 1))
          ELSE
            PeriodLengthTxt := COPYSTR(PeriodLengthTxt, 1, (I - 1)) + Char + COPYSTR(PeriodLengthTxt, (I + 1));
        END;
      END;
      Char := COPYSTR(PeriodLengthTxt, 1, 1);
      IF (Char <> '+') AND (Char <> '-') THEN
        PeriodLengthTxt := '-' + PeriodLengthTxt;
      EVALUATE(IOPeriodLength, PeriodLengthTxt);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeterminePeriodNo@1210190000(BasedOnDate@1100525000 : Date) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      FOR PeriodNo := 1 TO NoOfPeriods DO BEGIN
        IF (BasedOnDate >= PeriodStartDateArray[PeriodNo]) AND (BasedOnDate <= PeriodEndDateArray[PeriodNo]) THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempVendorTable@1210190002();
    VAR
      Vendor3@1210190000 : Record 23;
      Company3@1210190001 : Record 2000000006;
    BEGIN
      TempVendor.RESET;
      TempVendor.DELETEALL;

      Vendor3.COPY(Vendor);
      Vendor3.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF Vendor3.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempVendor := Vendor3;
          TempVendor.INSERT;
        UNTIL Vendor3.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      Company3.COPY(Company);
      Company3.FILTERGROUP(6);
      Company3.SETFILTER(Name, '<>%1', COMPANYNAME);
      Company3.FILTERGROUP(0);
      IF Company2.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          Vendor3.CHANGECOMPANY(Company3.Name);
          Vendor3.COPY(Vendor);
          IF Vendor3.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              IF NOT TempVendor.GET(Vendor3."No.") THEN BEGIN
                TempVendor := Vendor3;
                TempVendor.INSERT;
              END;
            UNTIL Vendor3.NEXT = 0;
          END;
        UNTIL Company3.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ProcessLedgerEntry@1100525001(VAR VendorLedgerEntry@1100525000 : Record 25) : Boolean;
    VAR
      BasedOnDate@1100525001 : Date;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(RemainAmtArray);
      CASE DateType OF
        DateType::"Posting Date":
          BEGIN
            VendorLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
            RemainingAmountLCY := VendorLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
            BasedOnDate := VendorLedgerEntry."Posting Date";
          END;
        DateType::"Due Date":
          BEGIN
            VendorLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amt. Due Date (LCY)");
            RemainingAmountLCY := VendorLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. Due Date (LCY)";
            IF VendorLedgerEntry."Due Date" <> 0D THEN
              BasedOnDate := VendorLedgerEntry."Due Date"
            ELSE
              BasedOnDate := VendorLedgerEntry."Document Date";
          END;
        DateType::"Document Date":
          BEGIN
            VendorLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amt. Doc. Date (LCY)");
            RemainingAmountLCY := VendorLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. Doc. Date (LCY)";
            BasedOnDate := VendorLedgerEntry."Document Date";
          END
      END;
      IF (RemainingAmountLCY = 0) AND (NOT (PrintType = PrintType::"All Entries")) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      NoDaysOld := ReferenceDate - BasedOnDate;
      IF NoDaysOld < 0 THEN
        NoDaysOld := 0;

      IF (RemainingAmountLCY <> 0) THEN BEGIN
        IF DeterminePeriodNo(BasedOnDate) THEN
          RemainAmtArray[PeriodNo] := RemainingAmountLCY;
      END;

      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
